1. The hotel is next to the business-World Trade Plaza, which is very convenient for eating and playing (I had dinner at "Zhuzhou Xunxian" diagonally opposite the hotel for two days)
2. The facilities, services, and hygiene are quite satisfactory. The shower water volume is very large and comfortable (Room 2617).
3. Small gym (2 treadmills, barbells, etc., suitable for 2-3 people to exercise at the same time).
4. Breakfast: It's quite satisfactory and can meet the dietary requirements of fitness people
Next time I go on a business trip, I will continue to stay at Junli Howard Johnson Hotel.
5. The hotel's location is very obvious, and the surrounding area is lively, so there is no need to worry about late-night snacks.
6. The room rate: I can accept it.
I have returned to Shanghai and will continue to book it next time I go on a business trip. Although it is about 30 minutes away from Zhuzhou West Road (the hotel is 2 km away from Zhuzhou Station), it is a satisfactory hotel. I am willing to comment and it is worth recommending.

msg:It was my first time in Zhuzhou. I booked a hotel on Ctrip. I was very surprised. I would like to share my feelings. The hotel is very new. It should have been opened not long ago. There is a small parking lot in front of the hotel. The doorman is very considerate and takes the initiative to help with the luggage. The front desk is smiling and serving like a butler throughout the whole process. Fruits are given. There are many elevators and they are very fast. The signs are very clear. The decoration style of the room is simple and warm, with dry and wet separation. I especially praise the overhead shower head. It is a bit exaggerated to describe it as a waterfall, but the amount of water is really cool! The room is managed by artificial intelligence Xiaodu, slippers, and toothbrushes. The quality is very good, which fully demonstrates the hotel's attentive service. Free afternoon tea is given, the tea set is exquisite, and the desserts and fruits are refined. The breakfast restaurant is not very large, but it is rich in variety and carefully matched with nutrition. There is also Hunan-style pepper fried meat. Goji berry chrysanthemum tea is also given when leaving the hotel. Overall, the hotel management is very attentive. It must be given a five-star rating. If I have to make some suggestions, it is that the waiters in the restaurant (some may have uncomfortable throats) will be more professional if they can wear masks or mouth supports. I wish the hotel to develop better and better!
